msg:Intercontinental was a very disappointing and weird experience this time. Although it is said that the hotel industry is very difficult during the epidemic, the facilities of Ningbo InterContinental are really bad. If the facilities do not meet the service standards, please stop providing them to customers.
Just got an upgrade to a lake view suite, which would have been to be grateful for. Entering the room, it is quite big, but the aura is not right, and a musty smell comes from the pavement. Going out from the living room is a huge terrace. When opened, it can run through the outer corridor of the whole building, so I don't feel very safe. The musty smell in the bedroom is heavier, the windows can't be opened, and after staying in the room for an hour, I still don't want to stay in such a room. The engineer of the hotel came to help look at the window of the bedroom, and told him that if he opened the window, he could only ask him to close the window... Then forget it, and insisted that the hotel change rooms. Switch to a small room, kid-style, with all sorts of chinchilla stickers on the walls. Although I never thought Chinchillas were cute, as long as the air is good and we feel safe, it doesn't matter. At night, I suddenly heard intermittent rumbling from the bathroom leading to the door in the room. I asked a hotel engineer to repair it, saying that it was caused by the blockage of the air conditioner filter. You should have cleaned the air conditioner filter. The hotel manager was panicking on the phone and said to help me change rooms, but I really didn't want to toss any more. Since the engineer thinks the problem has been solved, so be it. Until I went to bed, everything was fine, except that there was a detection light the size of an egg in the bathroom. When people walked over, the red light would flash and flash. Please note that it is the size of an egg. I thought it was weird so I stared at the light and it didn't come on. I don't stare, I walk around, and it continues to flash a few times, oh my god, what is this operation? Tired, go to sleep. Then I heard a loud noise in my daze, my God, is the air conditioner broken again. I tossed and tossed in bed, and there was a smoke detector on the top of the bed, with two tiny eyes that were blinking green. Look at the time, it's more than three o'clock, what can I do? Or just get up and drink some water, go to the bathroom, turn on the light in the room, and I'm instantly stunned. The loud noise of this drama turned out to be my suitcase smashed down! My god, my suitcase is opened and placed on the luggage rack. The box is not big, and it is not big enough to protrude from the luggage rack. Under normal circumstances, it is impossible to fall from it. As soon as I walked into the door, the red egg-sized light above my head began to flash again. My little heart started beating wildly. In the middle of the night, I was in a state of terror.

After 4 o'clock, through the slits of the curtains, yes, the electric curtains could not be closed tightly, there was a slit, I found that it was dawn, and I simply got up. Open the curtains, yo, the sun rises, a few swirls of morning glow are scattered in the blue sky, it is quite beautiful, just enjoy the sunrise.

I haven't slept well all night, and my hair has fallen out for a few days at home. How could this suitcase fall down so neatly is something I have never been able to understand.
